	8043.1.1 = { #Faith Militant Uprising
			effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { year = 8044 } }
				}
				any_vassal = { 
					set_character_flag = neutral
					clr_character_flag = supporting_king
					clr_character_flag = against_king  
				}
				set_character_flag = neutral
				clr_character_flag = supporting_king
				clr_character_flag = against_king
			}
		}
	8044.1.1 = { #Faith Militant Uprising
			effect = {
				any_vassal = { clr_character_flag = neutral  }
				clr_character_flag = neutral
			}
		}
	8050.1.1 = {death="8050.1.1"}
}

							modifier = opinion_targaryen_loyalist
							who = PREV
							years = 50
						}
						opinion = {
							who = PREV
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}	
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8197.1.1 = { #BR
		effect = {
			any_vassal = { clr_character_flag = supporting_king  }
			clr_character_flag = supporting_king
			clr_character_flag = warden_of_the_east

					opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion

					}
				}
			}
			d_daemon_blackfyres_host = {
				holder_scope = { 
					opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { year = 8197 } }
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8196.12.31={ 
		effect = {

				holder_scope = {
					ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV }
				}
			}
			clr_character_flag = against_king
			clr_character_flag = against_loyal_liege
			e_iron_throne = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			d_daemon_blackfyres_host = {
				holder_scope = { 
					remove_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = opinion_joined_cause
					}
					reverse_remove_opinion = {
						modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
						who = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
